<text>Unlike many BART stations, this one is relatively safe and clean. However, they do NOT time transfers between BART and Caltrain! If you time it wrong, or are just unlucky, you can easily get stuck waiting here for OVER AN HOUR for the next train, even during the middle of the day. Caltrain could easily time transfers, they just refuse for the sake of being stubborn (they insist it's BART's fault, BART insists it's Caltrain's fault). And there's almost nothing in the way of amenities. No food, no vending machines. No WiFi. No bathrooms on the Caltrain side (outside the BART paid area). Very few benches. No real shelter from weather. It's basically just a bare concrete slab. Oh, and if you're headed to the airport, you're supposed to transfer trains THREE times, have fun with that. Do yourself a favor, and just take an Uber or Lyft from the parking lot here.<//text><pics>None</pics>< response>

<rate>2< /rate>< Text>
We visited this store simply because it was on our way home from another location, but we were very disappointed. The produce section was under stocked. We buy mostly organic and needed a squash, but there was only 1 squash left which didn't look too good, so we didn't get it. There were also several spots for Taylor Farms pre-packaged salads, but most were empty. Stock was low on several other items as well.

At our local Albertsons, the bakery department gives free cookies to the kids. We went to the bakery department here to see if they do the same, and there was one worker busy helping somebody else. We waited about 10 minutes and finally gave up. The employee was still helping the first customer, never acknowledged us (I think her back was to us and the other customer the whole time), and no other employees showed up to help out. When we left, 2 more customers had lined up behind us.

We also avoided purchasing several dairy items because they felt too warm to the touch. I would compare it to taking something out of your fridge and letting it sit on the counter at least 1 hour. Even items toward the back felt warm. I looked around for a thermometer to check the temperature, but there weren't any that I could see.< /Text>
